## Analysis

The GT expression is:
`0.4770530111687279*P*sin(0.7760602430275763*t) + 0.44545499474048156*(1 - P/51.06128580599878)*P + 0.44545499474048156*P`

- `0.477053*P*sin(0.776060*t)`
- `0.445455*P - 0.445455*P²/51.0613`
- `0.445455*P`

Combining:
- P² term: `-0.445455/51.0613 ≈ -0.008725`
- P term: `0.445455 + 0.445455 = 0.89091`
- P*sin term: `0.477053*sin(0.776060*t)`
- No constant term

So GT = `-0.008725*P² + 0.89091*P + 0.477053*P*sin(0.776060*t)`

Now let me check candidates for a match. I need: `P²*a + P*b + P*c*sin(d*t)` or equivalent using cos with phase shift.

- c4 = 0

This matches the GT perfectly. ✓

- c4 = -π/2

This also matches. ✓
